  341. # [07:49] <seth> dbaron: unfortunately reftests heavily use images which behave differently before and after they've been "optimized" (for example, we may decide not to draw them as a raster image at all, but instead as a colored rect using graphics primitives)
  342. # [07:50] <seth> dbaron: and if they have to get redecoded when we take the reftest snapshot, we usually cannot optimize them at that time; we need to pump the event loop to do it (for various reasons)
  343. # [07:50] <seth> dbaron: so whether they got discarded and had to be redecoded means they may take very different drawing pathways
